## ⚡ EARLIER — 2026-06-26 **PHASE H · H5 increment 4 — FORTIFICATIONS DEPTH COMPLETE (D142), closing the locked D138 UG:G-fidelity modern-engine push.** This is a **D74 gameplay carve-out**, not presentation-only: the modern engine now has staged entrenchments (**rifle pits / hasty cover → full parapet → redoubt / earthwork**), facing-aware works (front strongest, flank reduced, rear bypass still matters), stronger/clearer prepared abatis when tied to own parapets/redoubts, visible 2D/3D earthworks, HUD status, a player charge-impetus commit lock, and H5-i3's swamp/town/fort arrays now feed the universal T0 cover/move hooks (no per-battle fudge). **NEXT = H2 reenactment-footage decision or Phase I/J polish; Q5 Chattanooga + Q6 USCT battles remain LAST.**

> **WHAT SHIPPED (D142):** `src/tactical/T13-engineering.js` now interprets `u.entrench` as staged works: early rifle pits/hasty cover, full parapet, then redoubt/earthwork. `fldEngCover(u, fromX, fromZ)` is stage + facing aware: frontal fire gets the earned bonus, flank fire is reduced, rear fire bypasses the works. Units that march off their own works lose the cover while the visible works fade. Abatis built by a brigade in its own parapet/redoubt is marked prepared, starts stronger, slows more, bites morale/disorder/fatigue harder, clears slower, and renders with clearer stakes/backing. 2D and 3D draw hasty/parapet/redoubt shapes; the HUD names the stage and front-cover multiplier; the end card teaches the Hess/Mahan fortification lesson.
>
> **CHARGE + TERRAIN SIM WIRING:** `src/tactical/T20-order-feel.js` adds the deferred player-only charge impetus lock: a 1.2s correction grace, then move/hold/queue/re-aim orders are refused until contact, target loss, fog loss, own rout, or own death. AI inline charges stay unchanged. `src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js` now wires D141 terrain through `fldCoverAt`/`fldMoveFactor`: fort strong cover + attacker friction, town hard cover + street friction, swamp soft concealment + major slow, with the old wall/woods/hill ladder retained. This is ONE universal combat model; no scenario outcome gate.
>
> **BUG-HUNT FINDING FIXED:** direct adversarial audit found the charge-lock predicate promised "rout/death releases" but did not test the charging unit's own state. ## ⚡ EARLIER — 2026-06-24 **PHASE H ("make it come to life") · H3-i2 — WEATHER + TIME-OF-DAY ATMOSPHERE: procedural sky/light re-tint (background · fog · sun · hemisphere) + rain/snow precipitation per a citation-grade per-battle `weather` hint; 2D + 3D. > **H3-i2 ships the next "come-to-life" increment — and gives every battle a sky matched to its history.** New `src/tactical/T17-weather.js` re-tints the 3D `scene.background`/`fog`/sun/hemisphere AND washes the 2D canvas to a resolved `{sky, time}` palette (sky ∈ clear/overcast/rain/fog/haze/snow; time ∈ dawn/morning/midday/afternoon/dusk), plus a procedural rain/snow `THREE.Points` cloud (the T16 shader pattern) + a 2D precip hatch, and a one-time accessible weather note via the existing role=status `fldScenarioBanner`. **The marquee: Antietam's pale warm dawn Cornfield ground-fog** (distant brigades fading into the mist, the objective still readable) — the one genuinely non-clear sky; the rest carry faithful time-of-day light (warm afternoons, cool mornings).
>
> **CITATION-GRADE DATA (research+verify Workflow, 18 agents).** The verifiers REFUSED to fabricate drama — Gettysburg `haze→clear` (Rev. Jacobs' instrument log: bright at the 2pm Pickett's-Charge window), Fredericksburg `fog→clear/afternoon` (the Rappahannock fog lifted ~10am, before the noon-to-dark assault — the note still teaches it), Shiloh `clear/morning` (the rain was OVERNIGHT), a misattributed Vicksburg source removed. **The honest finding: the "fog of war" at most of these battles was POWDER-SMOKE (already shipped via T16), not weather** — only Antietam's dawn fog is a real non-clear sky. Final hints (in `data/*.json`): bullrun1 clear/afternoon · malvernHill clear/afternoon · **antietam fog/dawn** · fredericksburg clear/afternoon · chancellorsville clear/morning · gettysburg clear/afternoon · shiloh clear/morning · vicksburg clear/midday(no-op) · chickamauga clear/afternoon.

## ⚡ EARLIER — 2026-06-23 **§12.3 THE ELECTION-SUPPORT RELIEF-BIND: a commissioned UNION political general (Banks/Butler/Sigel/McClernand) costs extra political capital to relieve before the 1864 vote — the bind Lincoln lived — relaxing once the verdict is in** (overnight run, D113)

> **The GM §12.3 command-politics keystone ships** (the bind the Commission move D109 was built around, now unblocked by the 1864-election state E4/D112). A commissioned POLITICAL general delivers his constituency's votes while he serves, so relieving him before the 1864 election forfeits that support: an ADDITIVE surcharge on his relief cost (`_cmdReliefCost`) that rises year over year toward the vote (1862<1863<1864) and FALLS to zero the moment `clock.resolved1864` is set. `surcharge = round((politicalValue/100)·windowByYear[year]·surchargeMax=14)`, bounded. A teaching tell on the active-general card names the constituency + the `+N capital` cost. Teaches §12.3 concretely: a fielded Banks both fields a low commandLeadership (49 vs Grant 87, D109) AND can't be cheaply dumped before November 1864. **Picked for an autonomous tick** over the frozen-loop E4-i2 (contained command-economy, no frozen-loop, no design fork); Aaron then reordered the queue — **E1 hinge-forks next, fantastical tier first.**

It is read ONLY by `cmdAppoint` (relief economy) + `_cmdActiveCard` (display) — **NEVER by `commandLeadership` or any combat/bridge/tick path** (grep-confirmed) → the bridge + 9 battles byte-identical by construction. ## ⚡ EARLIER — 2026-06-23 **Q12: THE DIVISION SUB-TIER — seat your generals into the DIVISION billets nested under each corps; a corps is only as good as its divisions** (overnight run, D110 — Codex code + Claude vetting/doc close-out)

> **The GM depth-chart's next rung is shipped** (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN §12.1 — Army → Corps → **DIVISION** → Brigade), built on the Q10 corps chart (D108). Beyond seating I–IV Corps, the President now SEATS pool generals into each seated corps's **3 DIVISION billets**, spending **political capital** (`C.clock.capital`, the existing GM currency). A division can be staffed ONLY under a SEATED corps (the real chain of command), so the depth chart is a TREE built top-down. Teaches that a corps was only as good as its divisions — A. P. Hill's "Light Division" and Hood's/Pickett's divisions were the cutting edge of Lee's corps, **as were the Union's hard-fighting divisions in Hancock's II Corps**.
>
> **⚠ PROVENANCE — this milestone was a CODEX HAND-OFF, closed out here.** The Q12 CODE + DATA + PROBE were authored in an interrupted Claude-Code session and **finished + committed (`7b64d2e`) + pushed by Codex** — a sound, builds-`GATE OK`, byte-identical-to-source feature — **but Codex ran NO adversarial bug-hunt and wrote NO doc trail** (D110 was absent from DECISIONS/HANDOFF/WAKE-UP/RUN-LOG/V1-CHECKLIST/RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN). This session is the **close-out**: ran the missing bug-hunt, fixed its one finding, and wrote the full doc trail. **No code reverted** — the commit is sound; the follow-up adds vetting + docs + one copy fix.
>
> **HOW IT REACHES THE FIGHT (byte-identical until you seat a division; D74/D94 no-fudge):** seated division commanders only add a small BOUNDED lift to `commandLeadership` — an INPUT the bridge already reads — via `_cmdDivLift` = clamp(Σ(`effDivRating`−64)×0.03, ±2). `effDivRating` = the general's GM OVR (carries the Q9 promotion) minus a `belowGradePenalty` (4) when his grade is below the **preferredGrade** — a division was a **Maj. Gen.'s** billet in BOTH armies (distinct from the corps tier where a CS corps was a Lt. Gen.'s), so any Brig. Gen. seated over a division leads stretched until promoted. The lift is deliberately SMALLER than the corps lift (cap 2 vs 4) so the hierarchy holds: **army ±17 > corps ±4 > divisions ±2.** No division seated → Σ over zero slots → lift 0 → the sandbox + all 9 battles identical to HEAD `7d86fcf`. **ONE BILLET PER MAN** (army/corps/division mutually exclusive; seating-higher clears the division); **vacating a corps CASCADES** (orphaned divisions stop contributing lift — enforced at the READ layer `cmdDivSeated`/`_cmdDivLift`, cleaned on load-sanitize). `cmd.divisions = {corpsIdx:{divIdx:id}}` rides the save (no `_SAVE_VER` bump); `cmdInit` sanitizes a tampered record on load. Writes ONLY `cmd.divisions` + capital (build-gate 4d scans `35-command.js`). NO RNG. `data/ratings.json` `divisionCommand` (Inferred + 2 sources: Glatthaar, Weigley).
>
> **Bug-hunt (5 diverse-lens Opus finders × default-refute verify + a completeness critic) → 4 lenses CLEAN, 1 confirmed LOW (FIXED):** the division teaching exemplars were **all-Confederate** (A. P. Hill / Hood / Pickett) while the rating mechanism is genuinely side-neutral and the sibling corps tier named both sides — the exact Lost-Cause over-celebration pattern CLAUDE.md #4 guards against. FIXED copy-only (byte-identical): added the Union counterpart (Hancock's II Corps divisions, Gibbon/Barlow) to the `divFoot` UI string + the `divisionCommand` `_note`. The save-tamper lens ran an 18-vector battery against `_cmdDivClean` (all sanitize correctly); the no-fudge lens grep-confirmed no combat path reads `cmd.divisions`; escaping confirmed safe.
>
> **Vet (offline gates GREEN; the headless `load` suite ENV-BLOCKED):** `GATE OK · no-fudge ✓ · citations ✓`; committed HTML **byte-identical to the source build**; `probe-command` **69/69** (+11 Q12 steps), **0 pageerrors**; `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; `t1probe` + `bootprobe` ok. **No tactical file is in the D110 diff** → the 9 battles are byte-identical to Q11 **by construction**. **ENV:** the strategic no-regression `load` battery (`probe-desk/ratings/camp/officers/field/oob` + the 9 battle probes) was blocked by the documented **THREE-CDN headless `load`-stall** (jsdelivr rate-limited the headless client after the first clean load; re-running the known-good `probe-command` reproduced the stall) — these probes share NO Q12 code path and were all GREEN in the Q11 vetting hours earlier. **The doc-trail + balance fix are committed in the close-out commit on top of `7b64d2e`.**

It fills the GM layer's central TEACHING keystone — §12.3's command-politics bind: these men were cheap to commission and weak in the field (Lincoln/Davis kept them for the factions, votes, and immigrant regiments they delivered, not their generalship), so once you appoint or seat one his low OVR drags the army's leadership (a commissioned Banks fields commandLeadership **49** vs Grant's **87**).

Gen., every string escaped, zero id-collision). **5 confirmed (2 MED + 3 LOW), ALL FIXED + the behavior-affecting ones probe-locked:** **(MED)** the commission economy was bypassable at the function level — `cmdAppoint`/`cmdSeatCorps`/`cmdPromote` accepted an un-commissioned pool officer via the widened `_cmdById` → a `_cmdByIdRoster`+`cmdCommissioned` guard added to all three (byte-identical for roster ids; probe-locked). **(MED)** a seated commissioned officer always rendered "I Corps" (string for-in key → `_cmdNum`→0) → `parseInt(kk,10)` (probe-locked). **(LOW)** the shared `cap` gate idiom passed NaN (`typeof NaN==='number'`; tampered-save only, pre-existing) → `&& isFinite(clk.capital)` at all 6 capital-gate sites + cmdAppoint debits the rounded `cap`. **(LOW)** `maxCommissions` fallback default 4→3. **(LOW)** a commissioned officer past his service window now reads muted "Commissioned · no longer in service" (was a green false "in your pool"). ## ⚡ EARLIER — 2026-06-23 **Q10: THE CORPS DEPTH-CHART — seat your generals into corps command over the Order-of-Battle tree; who you place (and whether his rank fits the billet) shapes how well the whole army fights** (overnight run, D108)

> **The GM depth-chart MOVE is shipped, built on the D106 OOB tree** (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN §12.1/§12.2/§12.4 — "an army version of waiver/trading/transfer"). Beyond appointing the ARMY commander (the existing `cmdAppoint` billet), a new President's-Desk **"The Corps Command — Depth Chart"** section lets the President SEAT pool generals into the army's CORPS billets (I–IV Corps), spending **political capital** (`C.clock.capital` — the existing GM currency, no new resource). Each billet shows its seated commander (name + grade + OVR + a below-grade tell) with a Vacate control, or "Vacant" + a pool `<select>` + a Seat control (gated on capital); a live read-out shows the net leadership the staffed corps add. Teaches real command organization — Lee's First (Longstreet) and Second (Jackson) Corps vs the Army of the Potomac's churning corps commands; the rout of Howard's XI Corps at Chancellorsville.
>
> **PICK RATIONALE (decide-&-log within the cleared NEXT menu):** chose the depth-chart MOVES (option A) over the symmetric AI-GM (option B, flagged [hard]) because A extends the proven `cmdAppoint`/`cmdPromote` spine over the D106 substrate and is byte-identical-until-moved like Q9; the new officer-slot/vacancy concept the derived T15 corps lacked is the `cmd.corps` slot map + a side-aware grade-fit.
>
> **HOW IT REACHES THE FIGHT (no new combat path; D74/D94 no-fudge):** seated corps commanders only add a small BOUNDED lift to `commandLeadership(C)` — an INPUT the bridge already reads — via `_cmdCorpsLift(C)` = `clamp( SUM over seated slots of (effectiveCorpsRating − 64) × perSlotWeight, ±liftCap )` (0.05 / cap 4). `effectiveCorpsRating` = the general's GM OVR (carries the Q9 promotion lift) minus `belowGradePenalty` (6) when his CURRENT grade is below the **SIDE-AWARE** preferred grade. It reaches combat ONLY through the existing `commandLeadership → bridge LEADERSHIP facet` pipe, NEVER the scoreboard (build-gate 4d scans `35-command.js` + `tactical/T15-oob.js`). The army commander still weighs most (~±17); the corps lift (±4) is a secondary modifier (§27).
>
> **THE SIDE-AWARE GRADE-FIT (historically precise; the Q9 synergy):** a US corps was a **Maj. Gen.'s** command, a CS corps a **Lt. Gen.'s** (the CS authorized the Lt. Gen. grade Sept. 18, 1862, promoting Longstreet/Jackson that Oct. to command the ANV's new corps). So on the shipped roster only CS **Stuart** (a Maj. Gen.) seats below grade over a corps; promoting him to Lt. Gen. (Q9) removes the penalty. `data/ratings.json` `corpsCommand`: `slots 4 · seatCost 3 · preferredGrade {US:"Maj. Gen.",CS:"Lt. Gen."} · perSlotWeight 0.05 · liftCap 4 · belowGradePenalty 6 · Inferred · 2 sources`.
>
> **BYTE-IDENTICAL until you seat a corps:** no corps seated → lift 0 → `commandLeadership` unchanged → the sandbox + all 9 battles identical to HEAD `2d11bd7` (a vacant billet contributes 0, NOT a penalty). `cmd.corps` rides the save (no `_SAVE_VER` bump); `cmdInit` sanitizes a tampered/imported record on LOAD (drop invalid slots/ids/dead generals/the army commander; one corps per general; array→{}). The army commander can't double-hold (excluded from the pool; `cmdAppoint` clears his corps). The seated commanders also NAME the player's DERIVED corps on the OOB board (pure display — the predicted edge is UNCHANGED; the enemy is never named; a "Garrison" node is never named).
>

Gen. grade date ("created Oct 1862") → corrected to the Sept. 18, 1862 authorization + the Oct. promotions + the Nov. 6 reorganization.

Intel is **fresh per engagement** (the scout record is keyed to the next-battle id → reverts to light when the battle changes). ## ⚡ EARLIER — 2026-06-22 **RATING SYSTEM LIVE DEV-TRAITS — a general's OVR now develops over the campaign, shaped by a hidden Madden potential ceiling** (overnight run, D105)

> **The last open item on the R-6 rating track is shipped** (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN §9-R-6 "reputation level-up → OVR still TODO" + D94-fork-#5 "Reputation→OVR dev-traits = LIVE in-campaign"). `cmdOnResolve` already evolved a general's reputation by battle outcome and `_cmdGenRating` (0.55·skill + 0.45·reputation) → `commandLeadership` already read it; D105 adds the **Madden DEV-TRAIT** that SHAPES that arc — a hidden potential **ceiling**, a **floor**, a development **rate** (rise vs fall), and an **attritionDrag** (the §15-R3 decline-with-heavy-attrition). **ACCURATE INPUTS, never an output gate (D74/D92)** — a dev-trait only shapes the general's REPUTATION (an INPUT the existing pipe consumes), it NEVER writes a casualty/winner; build-gate 4d now also scans `35-command.js` to make that structural.
>
> **THE KEYSTONE (byte-identical-when-off, the D104 pattern):** the `cmdOnResolve` seam is byte-identical for an UNASSIGNED general (or absent devTraits data) — the LITERAL pre-D105 path `clamp(cur+delta,5,98)`, rate 1, no drag (proven across ALL five outcome quadrants + both clamp rails). The deliberate, citation-grade change is the authored `data/ratings.json` `devTraits.assign` map (20 generals → one of **12 archetypes**). Ceiling/floor are RELATIVE to the seeded start (`devTrack.start`, fixed); every archetype keeps `ceilingAbove≥5 & floorBelow≥5` so the pre-D105 win-raises/loss-lowers invariant holds for all. **D105 touches NO tactical code → the 9 battles are byte-identical by construction** (`git diff` confirms the change is `35-command.js` + the `devTraits` data + the gate + the probe only; the tactical layer never runs `cmdOnResolve`).

## ⚡ EARLIER — 2026-06-22 **RATING SYSTEM R-6 (citation-provenance) — the CATALOG-WIDE citation hardening + a permanent build-gate** (overnight run, D103)

> **The citation-grade non-negotiable is now machine-enforced, catalog-wide.** Before you can hand a brigade a combat-biting negative badge keyed to a documented flaw, that flaw must be properly sourced — so this milestone shipped the prerequisite to R-6's negative-badge assignment. **An audit found the "Verified-with-<2-sources" debt was NOT just badges (the logged D98–D101 framing) — it was 47 records across SIX data files** (badges 13 · personas 2 · weapons 9 · artillery 9 · engineering 8 · terrain 1 · cabinet 5). All now carry **≥2 independent, real, web-verified sources**. PURE METADATA + a little teaching-card text → **byte-identical sim** (all 10 deterministic battles IDENTICAL to committed HEAD `5b12916`; **no numeric combat field touched**, bug-hunt-confirmed).
>
> **THE KEYSTONE — a permanent build-gate (`tools/build.mjs` gate 4e):** recursively scans every `data/*.json`; any record whose `prov`/`provenance` is "Verified" (matched **trim+case-normalized on EITHER key** — so a `"Verified "` whitespace/case variant OR an `Inferred`-masks-`Verified` pairing cannot erode it) carrying a `sources`/`src` array of <2 → `die(5)`. **Verified firing on all 47 before the fix; passes after** (`GATE OK · parse ✓ · hex ✓ · collision ✓ · no-fudge ✓ · citations ✓`). The ~72 long descriptive forms ("Verified specs (…)", "Verified (high) — …") cite inline in prose and trim-lowercase to ≠ "verified", so they stay out of the structured gate **by design**. This mirrors the 4d no-fudge wall: a non-negotiable made un-erodable by the build.
>
> **THE CITATION WORKFLOW (the ultracode pattern):** 15 Opus agents — 7 domains → per-domain finders → **default-refute** adversarial verifiers → a completeness critic; sources **web-checked**; discipline = NEVER fabricate, **downgrade-to-Inferred over guess**. **Zero fabrication** (critic-confirmed); all citations real/on-claim/independent. Two judgment calls: **`beloved` held *Inferred*** (its solid cite is Symonds 1997 on Cleburne; the obvious Lee source Freeman 1934 is Lost-Cause-tinged and held out); **`grand_charge` upgraded *Verified*** (Stewart 1959 · Hess 2001 · Sears 2003). Anti-Lost-Cause cut both ways: `feared`'s 2nd cite swapped Wyeth 1899 (hagiography) → **Hurst 1993**; the negative badges on real men carry the firmest pairs (Sears+Rafuse, Marvel+O'Reilly, Cozzens+Daniel, McMurry+Sword). **Accuracy fixes folded in:** the Fredericksburg cover card's "almost impregnable, and a deathtrap" was **misattributed to the NPS** (traces to a fan site) → paraphrased; `massed_battery` note dropped Pelham; `earned_in_blood` → "14 of the 16 (Army)"; Springfield/art-cs-handicap precision softened.

## ⚡ EARLIER — 2026-06-22 **RATING SYSTEM Q9 — the GM PROMOTION economy (the first depth-chart MOVE: promote · multi-currency · merit gate)** (overnight run, D102)

> **The first real GM *move* beyond appoint/relieve is shipped.** On the President's-Desk Command tab there is now an **"Officer Corps — Promotions"** section: the President promotes a general one grade up a clean strategic ladder (**Brig. Gen. → Maj. Gen. → Lt. Gen. → General**), spending a **multi-currency** budget — **political capital** (`C.clock.capital`, the primary, shared with relief/appointment) **+ a NEW seniority pool** (`cmd.seniority`, accrues over the campaign, capped) — and **merit-gated** by reputation. PURE INPUT-SEEDING + display, **byte-identical until the player promotes** (sandbox + all 9 battles proven byte-for-byte identical to committed HEAD `fc1d251`). Built on the existing `cmdAppoint`/`_cmdReliefCost` spine + the R-5 `fldPromotePerson` latent-command concept; entirely in `src/35-command.js` (the "Q9 (D102)" block) + a `promotion` config in `data/ratings.json`.
>
> **THE MERIT GATE (the honest history, the keystone):** each target grade carries a reputation **meritBar**. EARNED (rep ≥ bar) → a confidence bump (+3 rep); ABOVE merit (rep < bar) → a ×1.8 capital surcharge **+ a jealousy reputation HIT (−4)**. Because OVR = 0.55·skill + 0.45·reputation, **over-promoting a favorite past his record can LOWER his OVR** — rank without merit doesn't make a good commander (teaches the real command politics Lincoln navigated; anti-Lost-Cause: merit, not grade, is competence). Leapfrogging a passed-over senior adds a seniority surcharge.
>
> **HOW IT REACHES THE FIGHT (no new combat path, no fudge):** a promotion lifts the general's effective skill by a small **BOUNDED** amount — `_cmdPromoteSkillLift` = (rankBase grade-delta × 0.92), clamped to **≤6** — added inside the EDITED `_cmdEffectiveSkill(gen, C)`, which flows ONLY through the existing `_cmdGenRating → commandLeadership →` the bridge LEADERSHIP facet (an INPUT the sim already reads; `commandMarginEdge` reads aggression/caution, untouched). `cmdPromote` writes ONLY `clk.capital`/`cmd.seniority`/`cmd.promotions`/`cmd.reputation` — **never the scoreboard** (D74/D94 wall). **0 lift when un-promoted → every pre-Q9 reading byte-identical** (live-sanity proven: a promotion stores "Lt. Gen.", lifts commandLeadership 79→80; the un-promoted skill reads identical with/without C for all 20 generals).
>
> **New fns (`src/35-command.js`):** `_cmdPromoCfg`/`_cmdRankBase`/`_cmdBaseGrade`/`_cmdGradeIdx`/`_cmdNextGrade`/`_cmdCurrentGrade`/`_cmdPromoteSkillLift`/`_cmdLeapfrogged`/`_cmdPromoteInfo`/`cmdPromote`/`_cmdPromoRow`/`_cmdPromotionsHTML`/`_cmdNum`; EDITED `_cmdEffectiveSkill(gen,C)` (+lift), `cmdInit` (seeds + load-clamps `seniority`, seeds `promotions`), `cmdOnResolve` (accrues `seniority` — invisible/byte-identical), `cmdRenderTab` (+section), `cmdWireTab` (+promote buttons); call sites `_cmdGenRating`/`cmdActiveTraits`/`_cmdActiveCard` now thread C. **Data:** the `promotion` block in `data/ratings.json` (ladder · meritBar · capitalCost · aboveMeritMul · seniority{CostBase,Leapfrog,Start,PerTurn,WinBonus,Cap} · earnedRepBonus · aboveMeritRepHit · skillLiftWeight · skillLiftCap · topCommandPreferredGrade).
>
> **Bug-hunt (7 Opus agents: 4 diverse-lens finders × default-refute verify + a completeness critic; 2 raw → 2 confirmed + 1 actionable critic gap, ALL LOW + LATENT; 0 HIGH/MED; critic: "SOUND, may commit — no-fudge/byte-identity/bounding/determinism/no-exploit all hold; no HIGH/MED missed").** ALL 3 fixed: (1) `cmdPromote` gated on `round(capital)` but spent raw → now debits the rounded `cap` (one lens; byte-identical under integer paths); (2) `_cmdBaseGrade`'s unrecognized-rank fallback "Maj. Gen." would over-grade a future non-named officer onto the General ladder → now "Brig. Gen." (lowest; hardens the deferred depth-chart path); (3) `cmdInit` now re-clamps a tampered/stale out-of-band `seniority` to the cap on LOAD. The critic's 4th note (the two `diag-classic` 404s) is the pre-existing documented tolerated asset-layer noise, not Q9.
>
> **Vet:** GATE OK (no-fudge ✓); `probe-command` **25/25** (9 new Q9 steps incl. the save-tamper LOAD re-clamp + the byte-identity micro-assert); **byte-identity harness IDENTICAL for all 10** vs committed HEAD `fc1d251` + Q9 live sanity (0 pe); `probe-ratings` 19/19 + `probe-desk` 13/13 + `probe-camp` 8/8 + `t1probe` 14/14 (0 pe each); `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; `bootprobe` ok; `wcag-auditor` 0 AA failures (fixed the new warning text `#c2502e`→`#d66040`, 4.51:1). **ENV:** the `load` suite stalled intermittently on the THREE-CDN headless load (documented gotcha — cleared by a fresh threaded server + retry); the `domcontentloaded` byte-identity harness (`.tmp/q9-verify.mjs`, base `.tmp/q9-base.html` = `git show HEAD:civil_war_generals.html`) is the authoritative no-regression proof.

## ⚡ EARLIER — 2026-06-22 **RATING SYSTEM R-5 — the PROSOPOGRAPHY SCALE-OUT (bulk per-person rows + lazy materialization + play-as-anyone)** (overnight run, D101)

> **The D93 "Soldier's Story" substrate the whole rating spine was built for is shipped.** A brigade can now be inspected down to its men, any person *materialized* + *promoted*, and a generated soldier carries a deterministic name + Inferred rating — all **PURE DATA + DISPLAY**, **byte-identical** (no shipped scenario assigns bulk persons; sandbox + all 9 battles proven IDENTICAL to committed HEAD `84c5e95`). Selecting a brigade now shows its **MEN OVR** (the men's prosopography mean) beside the R-2 combat OVR, with a provenance-hatched accent.
>
> **THE LAZY-MATERIALIZATION KEYSTONE (§8) — the whole point of R-5:** a brigade TOKEN carries ONE aggregate `fldMenMeanOVR(u,year)` (its men's mean OVR, derived **O(1)** from xp + arm-branch + year + a deterministic per-brigade-id jitter, clamped [20,88] — a brigade AVERAGE never reaches the Legendary individual ceiling). Per-person rows are **NEVER instantiated en masse:** `fldMaterializePerson(spec,year)` builds exactly ONE row on demand; `fldBrigadeMuster(u,n,year)` a **HARD-CAPPED (≤6)** representative sample (captain/sergeant/private from `data/ratings.json` `musterTemplate`) — **never `u.men` rows** (proven: a 100,000-man brigade still materializes 3). The mean is always recomputable, never the source of truth (so a future zoom-to-regiment is a roll-up of materialized rows).
>

## ⚡ CONTINUE HERE — 2026-06-22 **RATING SYSTEM R-4 — the X-FACTORS (the dramatic "in the zone" surge, inside the no-fudge wall)** (overnight run, D98)

> **The Madden layer now SWINGS a fight — provably without ever touching the scoreboard.** An X-Factor badge enters "in the zone" when its situational trigger fires and surges on ONE channel, hard-capped. Demonstrated: a single `foot_cavalry` badge on one CS sandbox brigade **flipped a deterministic US win into a CS win** (same seed), yet the total-casualty shift was only **17.2%** and the command aura peaked at **0.47 < the 0.9 wall** — the rating reaches the result EMERGENTLY through bounded inputs, never by writing `cas`/`victory`/`men`/`sev`.
>
> **`fldXFactorStep(dt)` (`src/tactical/T14-ratings.js`):** gated on `__FIELD.badges`; for each unit carrying an `rung:"xfactor"` badge (`_fldUnitXFactors`), `_fldXFactorInZone` tests activation (march_vigor=moving · his_offensive=moving/charging · ammo_low_defend=ammo<12 & not charging · last_stand_defend=holding & (low morale or a friendly routing within 220yd) · usct_assault/mass_assault=charging · flanking=cav & charging). In the zone it surges **ONE channel = the declared lever**: a NON-speed X-Factor sets `u._xfActive = fldRatingRealismCap(tier,"xfactor")` (arcade 1.45 / balanced 1.20 / historian 1.08); a SPEED X-Factor (Foot Cavalry / The Slows) sets `u._spdMul` only (capped [0.85,1.15]) and does NOT also surge the aura. One-shot ⚡ `fldAnnounce`+`fldScenarioBanner` (`_xfOn` rising edge); `_xfGlow` marker pulse; deterministic `_fldXfDecay`→1 out of zone. **NO RNG.** A unit with no X-Factor is wholly untouched → byte-identical.
>
> **`fldXFactorApplyCmd(u)`:** `u.cmdBonus = min(FLDO.CMD_BONUS_CAP, (cmdBonus||0)*_xfActive)` — pushes the summed aura toward the **0.9 wall, never beyond**; strict no-op unless active. Called in `fldSimStep` AFTER `fldOfficersStep` (aura summed first), gated on `badges` (NOT officers) so both surge channels share one gate.
>
> **Seams (`src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js`):** `fldSimStep` runs the surge + apply around `fldOfficersStep`; **`fldMoveFactor` clamps the COMBINED speed factor** (the `_spdMul` surge × the R-3 static speed-badge factor) to ONE documented band **[0.75,1.30]** (exactly 1 → skipped → byte-identical); `fld2dDraw` draws a guarded `_xfGlow` — a CVD-safe amber burst RING (the shape carries meaning) + a **vector-drawn** lightning bolt (no emoji-font tofu), `reduceMotion`-honored. **Data:** added `first_with_the_most` (Forrest, cav) → 7 X-Factors; none assigned to a shipped roster yet (R-6) → byte-identical.
>
> **Vet:** GATE OK (no-fudge ✓); `probe-ratings` **17/17** (the R-4 surge step + the NO-FUDGE REPLAY GATE: the surge bites + bounded + capped); the **`domcontentloaded` byte-identity harness IDENTICAL for all 10** (sandbox + 9 battles, R-4 build vs committed R-3 HEAD — the authoritative X-Factor-off no-regression proof); `tactical-visuals` 10/10 scenes 0 pe; `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; the 9 battle probes + field + logistics + bootprobe passed via `load` (when momentarily healthy). **⚠ ENV (still intermittent):** the standard `load` suite stalled on the THREE CDN this session — the systems probes (officers/command/presets/…) were `load`-blocked, but the byte-identity harness exercises the full `fldSimStep`→`fldXFactorStep`→`fldOfficersStep` path (officers ON) for all 10 and proves it byte-identical, covering their core concern. **Re-run them next session once `load` is healthy** (serve via ThreadingHTTPServer; if `load` still stalls, the durable fix = domcontentloaded+settle in the probe runner OR vendor THREE locally — a recommended small vetted milestone). **Bug-hunt** (23 Opus agents, 16 raw → 4 confirmed + 3 critic, 0 HIGH, all LATENT@R-6): all 7 fixed (combined-speed clamp; cmdBonus surge gated to non-speed [one channel/badge]; apply decoupled from officers; vector bolt; grand_charge prov→Inferred + dual-downside deferred-note); catalog-wide badge-provenance sweep logged for R-6.

> **Chickamauga is playable and verified — the bloodiest battle of the Western theater, the fourth multi-phase epic, built on the T8 engine.** A new **⚔ BATTLE — CHICKAMAUGA (1863)** main-menu button (rank 60, after Vicksburg) opens the side-choice card; command Bragg/Longstreet's army or Thomas's defense across three sectors in sequence: **P0 The Battle in the Woods (Sep 19)** — a confused meeting engagement in blind timber; the Union line holds the road (historical). **P1 Longstreet's Breakthrough (Sep 20)** — the Wood gap order pulls a US division out of line at the moment Longstreet's column strikes the Brotherton farm; the CS pours through and routs the right (the decisive **scoreWeight-3** phase). **P2 The Rock of Chickamauga** — Thomas holds Snodgrass Hill / Horseshoe Ridge until dusk, reinforced by Granger/Steedman, saving the army. Anti-Lost-Cause: **contingency over genius** (a staff blunder + a timing coincidence, not martial superiority) and **the squandered victory** (Bragg fails to pursue → the siege of Chattanooga → the November reversal).
>
> **Framing (decide-&-log, no fork):** the C2 "Chickamauga/Chattanooga" item = a matched PAIR of separate 3-phase epics (the Antietam/Gettysburg precedent), each its own milestone. **Top-level `attacker: CS` / `defender: US` across all 3 phases** (the Army of the Cumberland fought on the defensive) — the CS player is the offensive, the US player holds. This sets **Chattanooga up as the US-offensive MIRROR** (the next milestone; design brief at `.tmp/chattanooga-design.md`, which also banks the engine-grain lessons from this build). Universal gun model only; **no per-battle damage fudge** (D74).

> **Balance (AI-vs-AI, 32 seeds, deterministic):** P0 US-holds 32/32 (mutual bloodbath ~2,400 each); P1 **CS breakthrough 32/32** (US routed cheaply, US:CS ~5.1); P2 **US-holds 32/32**, CS attacker pays **CS:US ~3.0** (the Fredericksburg failed-assault lesson); **aggregate CS 32/32** (CS 3 / US 2). A human US player who closes the Wood gap in P1 **overturns** the battle (the alt-history hinge). The CS won the field yet **bled MORE in aggregate** (~70k vs ~63k / 8 seeds) — the costly-victory teaching, probe-guarded.

Gen.; Loring removed; gap-reporter flagged (Kellogg vs Bond); "River of Death" shipped only as disputed legend.

## ⚡ CONTINUE HERE — 2026-06-18 Custom Battle Builder C4 complete ✅ — single-phase authoring, import/export, slots, launch gate green

> **Custom Battle Builder C4 is built and verified.** New `src/tactical/T11-custom-battle.js` adds a first-class main-menu builder flow for player-authored real-time tactical scenarios. It covers scenario name/date/place, sides/briefs, objective, field size, terrain hills/woods/walls/markers, OOB units, artillery/gun counts, reinforcement/deployment timing, optional leaders, supply trains, teaching cards, provenance, JSON import/export, shareable JSON, and six local persistence slots.
>
> **Architecture decision:** C4 is intentionally **single-phase V1**. Phase authoring remains deferred until a UI for `phases[]` can be proven as safe as authored historical phase data. Custom scenarios do **not** enter `fldScenarioRegistry()`; `fldScenarioData(id)` only falls back to `fldCustomScenarioData(id)` for explicit `custom_...` IDs. That preserves the exact historical battle roster while still launching valid custom scenarios through the same single-phase `fldScenarioInit` data path. Field size is reset every launch via `FLD.BASE_FIELD_W/H`, then a scenario may apply `field.w/h` safely.
>
> **Validation guardrails:** required metadata, safe unique IDs, malformed/unsafe JSON keys, duplicate IDs, bounds and numeric clamps, objective placement, reinforcement timing, side ownership, leader attach ownership, realistic artillery crew counts (12-40 per gun), forbidden combat/damage keys, and `phases[]` are all blocked. Custom artillery uses the universal `guns` model only; no per-custom-battle damage fudge was added.
>
> **Focused probe:** `tools/probe-custom-battle-builder.mjs` verifies builder render, validation failures, valid scenario creation, export/import round trip, UI malformed-import rejection, slot save/list/load/delete, explicit custom-ID launch contract, universal gun model, field-size reset, no phase leak, no Classic `G.battle`, and no historical registry contamination. Current result: **9/9 steps ok, 0 fail**, with `tools/shots/probe-custom-battle-builder.json/png`.
>
> **Verification:** `node tools/build.mjs` → GATE OK; `node tools/probe-custom-battle-builder.mjs` → 9/9; `node tools/probe-tactical-roster.mjs` → 8/8; `node tools/probe-field.mjs` → 13/13; `node tools/probe-bullrun.mjs` → 15/15; `node tools/probe-malvern-hill.mjs` → 24/24; `node tools/probe-antietam.mjs` → 16/16; `node tools/probe-fredericksburg.mjs` → 22/22; `node tools/probe-chancellorsville.mjs` → 24/24; `node tools/probe-gettysburg.mjs` → 16/16; `node tools/probe-shiloh.mjs` → 29/29; `node tools/probe-officers.mjs` → 15/15; `node tools/probe-logistics.mjs` → 14/14; `node tools/probe-arms.mjs` → 23/23; `node tools/probe-presets.mjs` → 26/26; `node tools/probe-csplayer.mjs` → 16/16; `node tools/probe-campaign-link.mjs` → 16/16; `node tools/probe-tactical-visuals.mjs` → 6/6; `node tools/bootprobe.mjs` → ok=true with known/tolerated 404 resource console entries; `node tools/t1probe.mjs` → ok=true; `node tools/diag-classic.mjs` → Classic paints, nonBlank 346; `git diff --check` → clean.

## ⚡ CONTINUE HERE — run k (2026-06-16): **PHASE C-1.5 · THE UNIVERSAL ARTILLERY GUN MODEL ✅ SHIPPED + VETTED + PUSHED** → IMMEDIATE NEXT = ANTIETAM as the MULTI-PHASE epic (D74 #1/#2)

> **The D74 "universal-combat" artillery cleanup — the FIRST Antietam sub-milestone (do FIRST) — is complete** (DECISIONS **D75**). Fredericksburg's per-battle **"volume-of-fire proxy men"** fudge (the C-1/D73 batteries inflated `men` to 500/440/500 to fake the massed crest fire) is REPLACED by a CONSISTENT gun-count model used identically in every battle. Deliverable ≈**1749.6KB**.
>
> **✅ THE GUN MODEL (T5):** `FLDA.GUN_FIRE_WEIGHT` = 27 (men-equivalent fire-strength per gun, UNIVERSAL). `fldArtFireStr(u)` returns the fire-strength numerator (`fldResolveFire` divides by 1500): a battery with a GUN COUNT → `guns * 27 * clamp(men/maxMen)` (rated fire from the gun count, crew-scaled so a battery fades smoothly as cannoneers fall); infantry / arms-off / a LEGACY no-`guns` battery → `u.men` EXACTLY as before. `guns` carried data→unit via `fldMakeUnit` (T0) + `fldBrSpec` (T1); wired at `fldResolveFire`'s `strF`. CALIBRATED so a 6-gun battery → 162 ≈ Bull Run's realistic 160-men/6-gun Griffin & Ricketts → the model REPRODUCES the existing batteries (consistent, not merely gated). The gun count is army-size-invariant "hardware" (strategic strength flows through the Cannon-Corps `_canisterScale`, not raw volume — documented).
>
> **✅ BYTE-IDENTITY:** the gun path is reached ONLY by a battery declaring `guns` (Fredericksburg's 3 crest batteries); every baseline has none → `fldArtFireStr` returns `u.men` → byte-identical. **field 13 · bullrun 15 · fog 13 · autopause 13 · ai 15 · campaign-link 16 · officers 15 · logistics 14 · presets 26 · csplayer 16 · arms 23** — all byte-identical, 0 pe; bootprobe ok; t1probe 14; diag-classic **346**.
>

The CS edge EMERGES from the wall's cover + the massed gun count + the cautious-attacker-dies-exposed geometry. Bug-hunt: **0 confirmed finder bugs + 5 critic gaps ALL FIXED** (the `u.men0` probe typo → maxMen; a battery-survival guard; a crew-scaling assertion; the campaign-semantics + legacy-HUD notes). ## ⚡ CONTINUE HERE — run k (2026-06-15): **PHASE B-3 · IN-BATTLE LOGISTICS ✅ SHIPPED + VETTED + PUSHED** → NEXT = B-4 distinct arm roles

> **✅ B-3 — supply trains + resupply + exhaustion:** each side fields a rear **ammunition train** with a finite **reserve**; a DISENGAGED brigade within reach refills (draining the reserve); a brigade OUT of cartridges holding the objective fires dry → bayonet (the 20th Maine); a SPENT brigade (fatigue>84) drags. The **attacker's train sits far behind its start line** (it outruns its supply) and the **defender's just behind the objective** → balance-neutral. **Ties strategic supply:** the reserve scales with `bridgeArmy().supply`; a raid-supply order cuts the enemy's. Gated + BYTE-IDENTICAL behind `__FIELD.logistics` (the 7 baselines + officers set sticky `_logisticsOff`).
>
> **THE FOG FIX (the headline — a HIGH bug-hunt finding, surfaced to Aaron):** with **fog ON**, logistics first INVERTED "fog aids the defender" (D58/D64) — Bull Run AI-vs-AI fog-ON **CS 8/8 → 0/8** (under fog the attacker cycled fresh brigades to its safe far-rear train and out-sustained the long fire-trade). Aaron's first pick (a defender's-depot rule) provably did nothing (the defender wasn't the ammo-constrained side); the fix that works (Aaron-approved) is **choking the ATTACKER's resupply under fog** (`ATK_FOG_RESUPPLY`=0 — an attacker advancing blind can't run its trains forward). **Result: logistics is balance-NEUTRAL in BOTH fog states — fog-OFF CS 5/8, fog-ON CS 8/8** (each = the no-logistics baseline; fog-aids-defender preserved). A FOG REGRESSION GUARD probe step locks it.
>

> **IMMEDIATE NEXT = the STRATEGIC ARC, charter-expanded (§7 item 2 / AUTONOMOUS-RUN §2).** **S2** = the FULL historical cabinet (§8.22) + one-line-rec/delegate/why advisor UX (§8.54) + 3-layer morale (§8.61; public-will-decides-late §8.67) + the 1864 election + the press/public-opinion system (§8.57) + command: appoint/promote/relieve generals (§8.58) + emancipation as a dated decision (§8.27) + civil-liberties dilemmas (§8.62) + named generals (§8.24) + the curated home-front event deck (§8.25). **Content may be recoverable via the cached s2-content-research workflow — see `AUTONOMOUS-RUN.md` §7 item 7** (else re-run a fresh advisor+decision-card research workflow). Then S3 alt-history · S4 education/codex/tutorial/WCAG-AA · S5 victory + graded report + Reconstruction · content systems · theaters · tactical P0–P5.
>
> **Full morning summary: `WAKE-UP.md` (root).** To run it: fresh chat → paste the `START-HERE.md` kickoff prompt → it loads `AUTONOMOUS-RUN.md` §2 (A1–A6 ✅, S2 next) + D42–D48 → continue the §3 loop at S2. Everything is on disk and pushed.

# HANDOFF — "The Civil War" — MASTER new-chat handoff (run h → next build)

**Written 2026-06-13 (run h, Opus 4.8). THE single entry point for the next session.** Personal project — NOT MJI. Full autonomy, Ultracode on, $0/free-CC0, build bar 200/100. **To start the next chat: paste the §PASTE block at the bottom.** Everything else here orients you.

---

## 1 · THE PROJECT IN ONE PARAGRAPH
"The Civil War" is becoming **the definitive teaching wargame: Ultimate General: Gettysburg's combat FEEL + Paradox-grade strategic DEPTH + a museum's historical RIGOR** — all three, no compromise. You are the **President (Lincoln or Davis)** running the entire war (economy, politics, diplomacy, morale, generals, the home front) AND commanding the battles in a real-time, gridless, drag-to-maneuver tactical engine — wrapped in a PhD-level history + alternate-history teaching layer where scholarly consensus is the *favored-but-not-guaranteed* path. **The governing design law (Aaron's central tension, resolved): the simple low-micro UG:G battle is the always-fun CORE that stands alone; ALL depth is optional — auto-managed by characterful advisors, delegable per-domain, preset-gated, fluidly dial-able; education is ambient, never blocks play, and confers real in-game mastery (so learning and fun pull the SAME direction).** One engine must serve the pure-battle player, the grand-strategist, and the PhD-historian simultaneously.

## 2 · WHERE THINGS STAND (run h, verified)
- **Classic (hex, turn-based) is FROZEN/finished** — the complete hex lineage + its 3D-skin "Modern." NEVER regress it (`tools/diag-classic.mjs` every splice).
- **Shipped + GPU-verified this run (all reusable):** procedural unit motion; **131 real PD-photo leader portraits** (`assets/portraits/`, license-gated, side-split for Anderson/Gregg) with a closure refactor + upgraded engraving fallback; a fuller period UI pass (drawn order-icons, engraved frames, brass portrait mat). Plus the inherited cinematic 3D foundation (PBR terrain, HDRI, ACES/bloom post-FX, weather, props, camera) and the adaptive period audio score.
- **The shipped "Modern" is only a 3D re-skin of the hex-turn engine** — it does NOT play like UG:G. The real-time tactical engine + the grand-strategy owner-mode are **NOT built yet** — that's the next work.
- **DESIGN: 63 decisions LOCKED** across a 35-round popup design session (Aaron). Fully captured in `GRAND-STRATEGY-PLAN.md` (Parts I–III). **No new-engine code written yet** — the next chat builds from the spec.

## 3 · THE DOCS (read in this order — you have zero prior context)
1. **`GRAND-STRATEGY-PLAN.md`** — THE DESIGN LAW. All 63 locked decisions: Part I (rounds 1–10: player/economy/executive/morale/alt-history/upgrades/education/victory/modes/first-build), Part II (rounds 11–20: diplomacy/slavery/politics/naval/map/generals/soldiers/intel/events/replay), Part III (rounds 21–33: **the depth↔simplicity balance** + presentation), §27 **the balance principle**, §13/§24/§28 decision indexes.
2. **`HISTORICAL-DATA.md`** — citation-grade content (211KB, 18-agent research): First Bull Run full OOB (Union + CSA), weapons/ballistics with ranges, USCT (structure/battles/criticism), the historiography framework, PD image sources. Feeds OOBs, weapon stats, debate cards, the codex.
3. **`MODERN-UGG-PLAN.md`** — the real-time tactical battle engine spec (built SECOND, after the strategic layer).
4. **`RUN-LOG.md` §"run h"** — what shipped + the pivot + this design session; skim §"run g"/§"run f" for the 3D foundation.
5. **`REVIEW-QUEUE.md` top** + **`GRAPHICS-RUN-CONTINUE.md` §TOOLCHAIN/GOTCHAS** — the splice/gate/real-GPU-shot toolchain + the bare-name-globals / async-THREE / override-by-redeclaration lessons.

## 4 · ARCHITECTURE DECISION (run h — important)
**Modularize via a zero-dependency build step.** The scope (50–100k+ lines) outgrows the single 14k-line file. Author the new engine in **source modules**; a tiny **node concat script** assembles the one shippable `civil_war_generals.html` (keep the $0/portable/open-and-play deliverable + `play.command`). Set this up FIRST in S0. Classic + the existing engine stay intact through the transition (move them into the build later, carefully, or keep the current HTML as the base the build appends to). Gate the BUILT output (parse/hex/Classic-regression). This replaces the append-only-single-file splice model for new work — but the gate discipline carries over.

## 5 · BUILD ORDER & PHASES (Aaron: STRATEGIC-FIRST, confirmed twice)
**Phase group S (grand-strategy owner-mode) FIRST, then phase group P (real-time tactical).** Battles use the EXISTING engine via a clean bridge until the UG:G engine swaps in.
- **S0 — scaffold:** set up the module/build system; expand the War Department (`G.campaign.{clock,muster,warroom}`) into the President's-desk shell (period war-room UI); strategic-turn loop; save. Layered scenario onboarding (start ~1861, limited toolset).
- **S1 — economy** (full asymmetric model + finance/inflation/blockade).
- **S2 — executive decisions + 3-layer morale + the 1864 election; the advisor/cabinet system** (the linchpin: auto-manage + recommend + TEACH, per-domain delegation).
- **S3 — alt-history engine** (tiered divergence + hinge-points + emergent toggle + curated scenarios; deterministic-by-performance with consensus framing; the "your war vs history" tracker).
- **S4 — education layer** (multi-voice debate cards + deep-dives + codex from HISTORICAL-DATA.md; ambient teaching; difficulty/realism sliders; play-style presets; full a11y).
- **S5 — victory/defeat** (asymmetric paths incl. **negotiated peace for both sides**, military-only hard-loss) + all campaign scopes; wire existing battles through the bridge → **playable full owner-mode war.**
- **THEN P0–P5** (`MODERN-UGG-PLAN.md`): the real-time UG:G tactical engine (First Bull Run vertical slice first), swapping in behind the bridge.
Each phase: gate + real-GPU self-verify (probes you READ) + Classic no-regression + left in a working, polished state (ship-quality iteratively).

## 6 · THE BALANCE PRINCIPLE (design law — apply to EVERY system)
The simple, low-micro UG:G battle is the always-fun core that works on its own. Every deep system is optional — auto-managed by characterful advisors, delegable per-domain, preset-gated, fluidly dial-able mid-campaign. Education is ambient, never blocks play, and confers real mastery (learning is rewarded by winning, not a chore-score). Presets + sliders let each player set their own balance. **If a feature forces depth on a battle-first player, it's wrong; if it denies depth to a strategist/historian, it's wrong.** (Full statement: GRAND-STRATEGY-PLAN §27.)

## 7 · TOOLCHAIN, GATES, GOTCHAS (proven — reuse)
- **Gates every change:** `.bak` → parse (`node --check` the built/extracted `<script>`) → invalid-hex grep `0x[0-9a-fA-F]*[g-z]` = 0 → collision-grep new fns = 0. With the new build step, gate the assembled output.
- **Real-GPU self-verify (READ the PNGs/probes):** `tools/shot-postfx.mjs`, `tools/shot-gpu.mjs`, `tools/shot-ui.mjs`, `tools/probe-motion.mjs`, `tools/probe-portraits.mjs`, `tools/bootprobe.mjs`, `tools/diag-classic.mjs`. Real GPU = **Intel UHD 617** via headed Chrome `--use-angle=metal`. A real-time sim/strategic loop needs an EMPIRICAL probe (sample state over frames), not just screenshots. Stale server: `lsof -ti tcp:8765 | xargs kill`.
- **Perf target:** smooth on the Intel UHD 617 at Auto tier; instancing/LOD/perf-tiers mandatory.
- **CRITICAL gotchas:** `G`/`HEX`/`PALETTE`/`THREE_BASE` are bare-name lexical globals (never `window.G`); THREE loads async (no top-level `new THREE.*`); override-by-redeclaration (last def wins); never a literal `*/` in a block comment; honor `reduceMotion` + `gfxQuality`; **NEVER regress Classic**; $0/free-CC0; Verified/Inferred provenance on all history.
- **Asset pipeline (historical run-H note; current top block supersedes live setup):** PD images via the run-h portrait pattern (Wikipedia REST summary → Commons license API PD-gate → download → `sips` resize). Extend to weapons/flags/USCT. Blender MCP remains available for future explicit 3D asset jobs (PolyHaven CC0 / Sketchfab), but Blender does not need to stay open unless a Phase-H asset task starts; free Hyper3D trial is drained.

- The **modes & toggles, all-play-styles** spine governs everything; **protect everything (no cuts)** is the scope ambition (build iteratively, but aim to deliver the full vision).
